        E.prototype.update = function(c, f, d) {
            var s, g;
            if (this.leftover) {
                for (g = 16 - this.leftover,
                g > d && (g = d),
                s = 0; s < g; s++)
                    this.buffer[this.leftover + s] = c[f + s];
                if (d -= g,
                f += g,
                this.leftover += g,
                this.leftover < 16)
                    return;
                this.blocks(this.buffer, 0, 16),
                this.leftover = 0
            }

            this.blocks(c, f, g),
            f += g,
            d -= g),
            d) {
                for (s = 0; s < d; s++)
                    this.buffer[this.leftover + s] = c[f + s];
                this.leftover += d
            }
        }

function po(e) {
    if (e.length % 2 !== 0)
        throw new Error(`Cannot convert ${e} to bytesArray`);
    const t = new Uint8Array(e.length / 2);

class pi {
    constructor(t) {

    }
    createKeypair() {
        return io.box.keyPair()
    }
    createKeypairFromString(t) {
        return {
            publicKey: po(t.publicKey),
            secretKey: po(t.secretKey)
        }
    }
    createNonce() {
        return io.randomBytes(this.nonceLength)
    }
    encrypt(t, n) {
        const r = new TextEncoder().encode(t)
          , o = this.createNonce()
          , i = io.box(r, o, n, this.keyPair.secretKey);
        return mc(o, i)
    }
    decrypt(t, n) {
        const [r,o] = wc(t, this.nonceLength)
          , i = io.box.open(o, r, n, this.keyPair.secretKey);
        if (!i)
            throw new Error(`Decryption error: 
 message: ${t.toString()} 
 sender pubkey: ${n.toString()}

        return new TextDecoder().decode(i)
    }

            publicKey: oi(this.keyPair.publicKey),
            secretKey: oi(this.keyPair.secretKey)

function qc(e) {

        throw new lr(`Wrong address ${e}. Address must include ":".`);
    const t = e.split(":");

        throw new lr(`Wrong address ${e}. Address must include ":" only once.`);
    const n = parseInt(t[0]);
    if (n !== 0 && n !== -1)
        throw new lr(`Wrong address ${e}. WC must be eq 0 or -1, but ${n} received.`);
    const r = t[1];
    if ((r == null ? void 0 : r.length) !== 64)
        throw new lr(`Wrong address ${e}. Hex part must be 64bytes length, but ${r == null ? void 0 : r.length} received.`);
    return {
        wc: n,
        hex: Zc(r)
    }
}
function Yc(e) {

            n ^= 4129)
    }
    return new Uint8Array([Math.floor(n / 256), n % 256])
}

                case a.PATTERN001:

                    }
                    ;
                case a.PATTERN010:
                    return function(x, Q) {
                        return Q % 3 == 0
                    }
                    ;
                case a.PATTERN011:

                        return (x + Q) % 3 == 0
                    }
                    ;

                    }

                    }
                    ;

                        return (x * Q % 2 + x * Q % 3) % 2 == 0
                    }
                    ;
                case a.PATTERN111:

                        return (x * Q % 3 + (x + Q) % 2) % 2 == 0
                    }
                    ;
